			}
		}

		// Modifiers
		//lava goes through invulnerability
		//if invulnerable, you can't be healed
		"Modifiers"
		{
			"heal_aura"
			{
				"Passive"      "1"
				//"IsHidden"      "1"
			
				"Aura"            "autoheal"
				"Aura_Radius"     "%range"
				"Aura_Teams"      "DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_TEAM_BOTH"
				"Aura_Types"      "DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_HERO"

				"ThinkInterval"  "0.1"
				//modifier is destroyed on leaving the aura
				"OnIntervalThink"
				{
					"ApplyModifier"
					{
						"ModifierName"  "autoheal"
						"Target"     "TARGET"
					}
				}
			}

			"autoheal"
			{

				//"Passive"         "0"
				"IsDebuff"    "0" 
				//apply another "OnIntervalThink" to make it heal at every interval
				//modifier stays attached even if duration is set to shorter than the interval
				"ThinkInterval"  "0.1"
				"OnIntervalThink"
				{
					"Heal"
					{
						"HealAmount"		"10000"
						"Target"			"TARGET"
					}
					"RemoveModifier"
					{
						"ModifierName"  "autoheal"
						"Target"			"TARGET"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
